In this course, professional photographer and trainer Hollin Jones shows you how to quickly and easily import, organize, edit and export your photos using Lightroom.\r\n\r\nHollin starts his presentation with a look at Lightroom’s interface and its basic features. He explains how to navigate Lightroom’s single window interface, how to use the different view modes, and he shares useful keyboard shortcuts that are guaranteed to improve your workflow. You also learn how to import photos, and how to organize large photo collections using keywords and multiple libraries.\r\n\r\nNext, Hollin dives into the Develop mode where you learn how to edit your pictures. He reveals how to add depth and intensity to your photos, by adjusting the tone curve, color balance, saturation, luminance and other parameters. Hollin also share some advanced Photoshop-like techniques, such as spot removal, creative radial filtering, the adjustment brush, and more. The final chapters of the course cover exporting your work, and protecting your images from copyright infringement with watermarks.\r\n\r\nSo sit back and watch this 19-tutorial info-packed course.
